                       Come stay at my newly remodeled apartment right near downtown! 42" LED 1080p TV/BluRay/Bose Strereo &amp; quick drive to Redbox -- No Cable 2mi (9min) to Downtown Core/LA Live/Staples Ctr/Dodgers Stadium/LA Convention Ctr
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2237">
                       Come stay in this entire, private apt by Downtown LA. You'll be central to LA's major metros &amp; freeways, &amp; super close to LA's attractions like the Staples &amp; LA Convention Centers, LA Live, NOKIA &amp; USC. Great for tourists or students. This apartment is ideal friends or family looking for a very affordable and easy alternative to the smaller and more expensive rentals in the immediate area. ★ DESCRIPTION The apartment has a queen bed. The unit also features free high-speed wireless Internet and a new TV with Blu-Ray DVD player and Antenna reception. You can stream entertainment from your computers (there's a Redbox down the street) Kitchen - This is a FULL sized kitchen which includes a sink, fridge, microwave and gas stove top. Bathroom - This is a FULL sized bathroom with a shower, tub, sink, toilet, etc. Living Room - The living room features a brand new 1080p TV and BluRay player, and a new European style couch. ★ LOCATION It's just a 5 minute drive to LA Live, Nokia Theater and Staples Center. It's just 10 minutes to Dodger Stadium, and trendy Echo Park and ultra hip Silver Lake and Sunset Junction. ★ NEARBY DESTINATIONS Only a few minutes drive / cab to - - USC - Metro Red Line (which goes to Hollywood and Universal Studios) - Metro Gold Line (which goes to Pasadena) - Metro Blue Line (which goes to Long Beach) - The Big Blue Bus Rapid 10 (which goes to Santa Monica beach and Venice Beach) - Major Freeway systems, like Highways: I-110 and I-10, 101, I-5 ★ OTHER INFO - CHECK-IN / OUT - You can check in after 3pm and leave before 12 noon. The process is easy because we have a key lock box on the property so you can have a flexible schedule. - WIFI - High Speed Wireless Internet provided by Time Warner cable service - PARKING - Dedicated parking but it is a shared tandem with the guy next door, you'll have to knock on his door to get out sometimes. Remember I usually exchange keys in person and I'll show you around. Keep in touch of there are any questions I can answer for you! Westlake is super close to Silverlake DTLA and Echo Park (Silverlake is one of the moThis location is in the Westlake neighborhood in Los Angeles. Nearby parks include Parkview Playground, MacArthur Park and MacArthur Park, Los Angeles, CA. A 14 minute walk from the Metro Line.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="2238">
                       This location is close to all the things mentioned. However, don't get the idea it's easy to walk from place to place--there's not much in the immediate 1mi vicinity to walk to.
